 com / 0g314cxuqj neshnal medical bill (NMC) ko lekar doctoron main virodh badhata ja rahaa he
 Demonstrations against the bill were held in several institutions in the country, including Delhi's AIIMS and Safdarganj Hospital, besides PGI Chandigarh and Aligarh Muslim University (AMU)
 yah pradarshan ames se sansad bhawan tak yojit kiya gaya jisamen 10 hajaar se zyada doctoron ne bill ke kai praavdhaanon kaa virodh kiya
 According to this bill, there is a plan to implement the National Medical Commission body in place of the existing Medical Council of India
 bill kaa virodh indian medical association (IMA) bhi kar rahaa he
 After heavy protests by doctors across the country, the bill was sent to the Select Committee of Parliament by the government
 is bill main neshnal medical bill ke tahat chaar swytt board banane kaa praavdhaan he
 Their work will be to look at undergraduate and post graduate education, besides the recognition of medical institutions and the system of registration of doctors
 kamishan main sarkaar dwaara namit chairman or sadsy honge, jabaki bordon main sadasyon kaa chayan search cameti ke jariye kiya jayega
 It will be made under the supervision of the Cabinet Secretary
 panel main 12 purv or paanch chaynit sadsy honge
 Also, the bill proposes to conduct a license examination along with a common entrance examination
 sabhi snaatakon ko practice karne ke liye license pariksha ko paas karnaa hoga
 Through the bill, it is being ensured that institutions will not need permission to increase seats and start post graduate courses
 sarkaar kii ore se kaha ja rahaa he ki is bill kaa makasad desh kii chikitsa shiksha kshetra main badlaav laane ke alaava ise bhrashtachar or aniatik gatividhiyon se mukt karana he
 On the other hand, the IMA states that this will reduce the level of medical treatment in a big way and it will play with patient care and safety
 aadhunik chikitsa paddati ke tahat practice ke liye embibies kaa maanak bane rahanaa chahie
 In this bill, practitioners of Indian system of medicine including Ayurveda have been allowed to practice allopathy after doing a bridge course
 doctors iskaa bhi virodh kar rahe hai
 The IMA also objected to the provision of the bill that empowered management to fix fees for seats
 privet medical collejon main 15% siton kaa fees management tay karti thi lekin ab nae bill ke mutabik management ko 60% siton kii fees tay karne kaa adhikaar hoga
 The AIIMS Resident Doctors Association has also opposed this bill, calling this current bill against the poor, against the people and unacceptable

 If you follow these tips before then it is a good thing, but if you have not done it before, now is the time
 sef password- kisi bhi acount ke password main special kairactor or digits jarur rakhen
 Keep a combination of caps and small
 iske alaava kam se kam har chah maheene par password badalte rahen
 Anti Virus - Use premium anti virus and keep it updated always
 samay samay par apane computer or smartphone ko usase scan karte rahen
 Updates - Never ignore computer and smartphone updates
 kyonki companiyaan iske jariye security ptch detii hai jo aapke system ko surakshit rakhte hai

 Device Lock - Keep your smartphone or laptop locked at all times through a fingerprint scanner or PIN

 App Installation - Before installing any app in computer and mobile, check whether it is from the verified publisher or not
 iske alaava yah bhi dekhen ki wo aapke smartphone se koun koun si jaankariyaan hasil karegaa

 kyonki agar router hack hua to usase jude sabhi divaais ke trephic se password churaayaa ja saktaa he
 So keep strong passwords in it and do not tell the unknown
 email, powep or farji link -kisi bhi aise email main die gaye atachament ko na kholen jo puri tarah anjaan hon or farji lag rahe hai
 Because it is easiest for hackers to take control of your system through a link
 aise hi aap kisi pop ap vigyaapan or soshal media par viral ho rahe farji link ko open karne se bhi bachein
